summary\n\nThe cli_portify architecture is already fairly well decomposed, but the top-level CLI runner is still not wired to execute the 7-step pipeline end-to-end. The current codebase already has:\n\n- typed config and step result models\n- gate infrastructure for all 7 steps\n- contract builders for success/partial/failure/dry-run\n- Claude subprocess wrapper for steps 3-7\n- monitoring primitives: NDJSON event logging, timing capture, failure classification, markdown diagnostic reporting\n- convergence engine for step 7 iterations\n- step implementations for all 7 steps\n- prompt builders for all Claude-assisted steps\n\nWhat is missing at the top level is the orchestration layer that actually sequences steps 1-7, tracks overall status, invokes contract emission on exits, and integrates monitor/timing/event logger in a single execution loop.\n\n## 1. Data models in `models.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/models.py`\n\n### Imported shared pipeline types\nThis module imports these shared base types from `superclaude.cli.pipeline.models`:\n- `PipelineConfig`\n- `StepResult`\n- `StepStatus`\n\nImportant: `StepStatus` itself is not defined in cli_portify. It is imported from the shared pipeline package.\n\n### Enums\n\n#### `PortifyStatus`\nStep-level status enum:\n- `PENDING = \"pending\"`\n- `RUNNING = \"running\"`\n- `PASS = \"pass\"`\n- `FAIL = \"fail\"`\n- `TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"`\n- `SKIPPED = \"skipped\"`\n- `ERROR = \"error\"`\n\nThis is the primary cli_portify step status vocabulary.\n\n#### `PortifyOutcome`\nAggregate pipeline outcome enum:\n- `SUCCESS = \"success\"`\n- `PARTIAL = \"partial\"`\n- `FAILED = \"failed\"`\n- `DRY_RUN = \"dry_run\"`\n\nThis concept aligns with contract emission status, though `contract.py` defines its own `ContractStatus` enum separately.\n\n#### `FailureClassification`\nFailure taxonomy used for diagnostics and resume logic:\n- `TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"`\n- `MISSING_ARTIFACT = \"missing_artifact\"`\n- `MALFORMED_FRONTMATTER = \"malformed_frontmatter\"`\n- `GATE_FAILURE = \"gate_failure\"`\n- `USER_REJECTION = \"user_rejection\"`\n- `BUDGET_EXHAUSTION = \"budget_exhaustion\"`\n- `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT = \"partial_artifact\"`\n\n### `PortifyConfig`\nExtends shared `PipelineConfig`.\n\nFields:\n- `workflow_path: Path = Path(\".\")`\n- `output_dir: Path = Path(\".\")`\n- `cli_name: str = \"\"`\n- `skip_review: bool = False`\n- `start_step: str | None = None`\n- `iteration_timeout: int = 300`\n- `max_convergence: int = 3`\n\nInherited fields are not listed here explicitly, but `config.py` passes these into it via the base class:\n- `work_dir`\n- `dry_run`\n- `max_turns`\n- `model`\n- `debug`\n\nKey behavior:\n- `__post_init__`: if `work_dir` is empty or `\".\"`, it sets `work_dir = output_dir`\n- `resolve_workflow_path()`: validates workflow path and requires `SKILL.md`\n- `derive_cli_name()`: derives CLI name from folder name by:\n  - stripping `sc-` prefix\n  - stripping `-protocol` suffix\n  - replacing `_` with `-`\n- `check_output_writable()`: creates output dir if needed and validates it is a directory\n- `check_name_collision(existing_commands=None)`: checks built-in command collisions against:\n  - `install`\n  - `mcp`\n  - `update`\n  - `install-skill`\n  - `doctor`\n  - `version`\n  - `sprint`\n  - `roadmap`\n  - `cleanup-audit`\n  - `tasklist`\n- `to_snake_case(name=None)`: kebab to snake conversion\n- `results_dir` property: `output_dir / \"results\"`\n- `artifacts_dir` property: `output_dir / \"artifacts\"`\n\n### `ResumeContext`\nTyped resume metadata.\n\nFields:\n- `last_completed_step: str = \"\"`\n- `last_completed_step_number: int = 0`\n- `failed_step: str = \"\"`\n- `failed_step_number: int = 0`\n- `failure_classification: FailureClassification | None = None`\n- `re_run_required: bool = False`\n- `artifacts_preserved: list[str] = []`\n- `resume_command: str = \"\"`\n\nThis is present in the step result model, but current step implementations do not populate it much yet.\n\n### `PortifyStepResult`\nExtends shared `StepResult`.\n\nFields:\n- `portify_status: PortifyStatus = PortifyStatus.PENDING`\n- `step_name: str = \"\"`\n- `step_number: int = 0`\n- `phase: int = 0`\n- `artifact_path: str = \"\"`\n- `gate_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n- `iteration_timeout: int = 300`\n- `iteration_number: int = 0`\n- `review_required: bool = False`\n- `review_accepted: bool | None = None`\n- `failure_classification: FailureClassification | None = None`\n- `resume_context: ResumeContext = ResumeContext()`\n\nComputed property:\n- `is_resumable`\n  - returns `False` for `USER_REJECTION`\n  - otherwise returns `True` when status is `FAIL`, `TIMEOUT`, or `ERROR`\n\nSo current resumability logic is classification-based and intentionally excludes user rejection.\n\n### `ComponentEntry`\nRepresents one discovered workflow component.\n\nFields:\n- `name: str`\n- `path: str`\n- `component_type: str`\n- `line_count: int`\n\n### `ComponentInventory`\nProduced by step 2.\n\nFields:\n- `source_skill: str = \"\"`\n- `components: list[ComponentEntry] = []`\n\nComputed properties:\n- `component_count`\n- `total_lines`\n\n### `PortifyMonitorState`\nLive execution state intended for TUI rendering.\n\nFields:\n- `output_bytes: int = 0`\n- `output_bytes_prev: int = 0`\n- `last_growth_time: float = 0.0`\n- `last_event_time: float = 0.0`\n- `step_started_at: float = 0.0`\n- `events_received: int = 0`\n- `lines_total: int = 0`\n- `growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0`\n- `stall_seconds: float = 0.0`\n- `current_step: str = \"\"`\n- `current_iteration: int = 0`\n\nComputed property:\n- `stall_status`\n  - if no events:\n    - `<30s` => `\"waiting...\"`\n    - `>=30s` => `\"STALLED\"`\n  - if `stall_seconds > 120` => `\"STALLED\"`\n  - if `stall_seconds > 30` => `\"thinking...\"`\n  - else => `\"active\"`\n\nThis is only a state model; I did not find a renderer consuming it.\n\n## 2. Contract architecture in `contract.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/contract.py`\n\n### Contract status enum\n`ContractStatus`:\n- `SUCCESS`\n- `PARTIAL`\n- `FAILED`\n- `DRY_RUN`\n\n### `PhaseStatus`\nFields:\n- `phase: int`\n- `name: str`\n- `status: str = \"pending\"`\n- `steps_completed: int = 0`\n- `steps_total: int = 0`\n\nSerialized keys:\n- `phase`\n- `name`\n- `status`\n- `steps_completed`\n- `steps_total`\n\n### `StepTiming`\nThis is a contract-specific timing dataclass, different from the one in `monitor.py`.\n\nFields:\n- `step: str`\n- `duration_seconds: float = 0.0`\n\n### `PortifyContract`\nFields:\n- `status: ContractStatus = ContractStatus.FAILED`\n- `phases: list[PhaseStatus] = []`\n- `artifacts: list[str] = []`\n- `resume_command: str = \"\"`\n- `timing: dict[str, Any] = {}`\n- `step_timings: list[StepTiming] = []`\n- `gate_results: dict[str, str] = {}`\n- `error_message: str = \"\"`\n\nSerialization output keys:\n- `status`\n- `phases`\n- `artifacts`\n- `resume_command`\n- `timing`\n- `step_timings`\n- `gate_results`\n- `error_message`\n\n`__post_init__` populates default phases if omitted.\n\n### Default phases\nThe contract hardcodes 4 conceptual phases:\n\n1. `config-validation` — `steps_total=2`\n2. `workflow-analysis` — `steps_total=2`\n3. `spec-synthesis` — `steps_total=1`\n4. `review-convergence` — `steps_total=2`\n\nStep-to-phase mapping:\n- step 1 `validate-config` -> phase 1\n- step 2 `discover-components` -> phase 1\n- step 3 `analyze-workflow` -> phase 2\n- step 4 `design-pipeline` -> phase 2\n- step 5 `synthesize-spec` -> phase 3\n- step 6 `brainstorm-gaps` -> phase 4\n- step 7 `panel-review` -> phase 4\n\n### Contract builder functions\n\n#### `build_success_contract(...)`\nMarks all phases:\n- `status = \"completed\"`\n- `steps_completed = steps_total`\n\nSets:\n- `status = success`\n- `resume_command = \"\"`\n- `timing = {\"total_seconds\": total_duration}`\n\n#### `build_partial_contract(...)`\nUsed for escalated partial completion.\n\nInputs:\n- `step_results`\n- `artifacts`\n- `step_timings`\n- `gate_results`\n- `total_duration`\n- `resume_step=\"\"`\n\nBehavior:\n- builds phase states from step results\n- optionally generates resume command\n\n#### `build_failed_contract(...)`\nUsed for failure exit paths.\n\nAdds:\n- `error_message`\n- optional `resume_command`\n\nThis is intended to satisfy the \"no null contract on failure\" rule.\n\n#### `build_dry_run_contract(...)`\nSpecial dry-run behavior:\n- phases 1-2 marked `completed`\n- phases 3-4 marked `skipped`\n- `resume_command = \"\"`\n\nNote: comment says phases 1-2 are \"config validation + deterministic steps\", but implementation is based on conceptual pipeline phases, not actual execution tracking.\n\n### Resume command generation\n`RESUMABLE_STEPS`:\n- `synthesize-spec` -> 5\n- `brainstorm-gaps` -> 6\n- `panel-review` -> 7\n\n`generate_resume_command(failed_step, suggested_budget=None)` returns:\n- `superclaude cli-portify run <workflow_path> --start {failed_step}`\n- appends `--max-convergence {suggested_budget}` when provided\n\nNon-resumable steps return empty string.\n\n## 3. CLI entry point and flags in `cli.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/cli.py`\n\n### CLI group\n- Click group name: `cli-portify`\n\n### Command\n- Subcommand: `run`\n\n### Positional argument\n- `workflow_path` as `click.Path(exists=True)`\n\n### Defined flags\n- `--output` / stored as `output_dir`\n  - output directory for generated artifacts\n- `--cli-name`\n  - overrides derived CLI command name\n- `--dry-run`\n  - validates and plans without executing Claude steps\n  - help text says halts after step 2\n- `--skip-review`\n  - skips interactive review gates\n- `--start` / stored as `start_step`\n  - resume from a specific step\n  - help example: `synthesize-spec`\n- `--max-convergence`\n  - default `3`\n  - maximum convergence iterations for panel review\n- `--iteration-timeout`\n  - default `300`\n  - per-iteration timeout\n- `--max-turns`\n  - default `100`\n  - max turns per Claude subprocess\n- `--model`\n  - default empty string\n- `--debug`\n  - flag\n\n### Current actual behavior\nThe runner currently does only this:\n1. builds config via `load_portify_config(...)`\n2. validates config via `validate_portify_config(config)`\n3. if validation errors exist:\n   - prints each as `Error: ...`\n   - exits `1`\n4. if `dry_run`:\n   - prints a dry-run execution plan\n   - returns\n5. otherwise:\n   - prints `cli-portify: pipeline execution not yet implemented (start=...)`\n   - exits `0`\n\nSo:\n- `--start` exists but is not yet wired to an execution loop\n- `--skip-review` exists and is carried in config, but top-level orchestration is not using it yet\n- actual pipeline sequencing is still deferred\n\n### Dry-run display\n`_print_dry_run(config)` prints:\n- workflow path\n- derived CLI name\n- output dir\n- total step count: `7 (Steps 3-7 require Claude)`\n- max convergence\n- iteration timeout\n\n## 4. Pipeline execution flow\n\nThere is no fully implemented top-level pipeline runner yet in `cli.py`, but the intended flow is very clear from the steps, contracts, gates, prompts, and convergence code.\n\n### Intended step order\nFrom `steps/__init__.py` and step implementations:\n\n1. `validate-config`\n2. `discover-components`\n3. `analyze-workflow`\n4. `design-pipeline`\n5. `synthesize-spec`\n6. `brainstorm-gaps`\n7. `panel-review`\n\n### Phase grouping\n- Phase 1:\n  - step 1 `validate-config`\n  - step 2 `discover-components`\n- Phase 2:\n  - step 3 `analyze-workflow`\n  - step 4 `design-pipeline`\n- Phase 3:\n  - step 5 `synthesize-spec`\n- Phase 4:\n  - step 6 `brainstorm-gaps`\n  - step 7 `panel-review`\n\n### Step dependencies\n- Step 1 validates config and environment\n- Step 2 consumes resolved workflow path and inventories source files\n- Step 3 requires `component-inventory.md`\n- Step 4 requires `portify-analysis.md`, also references `component-inventory.md`\n- Step 5 requires:\n  - `release-spec-template.md`\n  - `portify-analysis.md`\n  - `portify-spec.md`\n- Step 6 requires `synthesized-spec.md`\n- Step 7 requires:\n  - `synthesized-spec.md`\n  - `brainstorm-gaps.md`\n\n### Claude-assisted vs deterministic\nDeterministic:\n- step 1\n- step 2\n\nClaude-assisted:\n- steps 3-7\n\n### Actual subprocess orchestration in `process.py`\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/process.py`\n\n`PortifyProcess` is not a pipeline executor. It is a step-level subprocess wrapper around shared `ClaudeProcess`.\n\nWhat it adds:\n- dual `--add-dir` scoping:\n  - `work_dir`\n  - `workflow_path` if different\n- prompt augmentation with `@absolute/path` references to prior artifacts\n- captured stdout/stderr/timeout/duration result object\n\n`ProcessResult` fields:\n- `exit_code`\n- `stdout_text`\n- `stderr_text`\n- `timed_out`\n- `duration_seconds`\n- `output_file`\n- `error_file`\n\n`succeeded` means:\n- `exit_code == 0`\n- and not timed out\n\n### Prompt construction flow\nAll Claude-assisted steps use `prompts.py` builders with a shared `PromptContext`.\n\nEach builder supplies:\n- referenced input artifacts\n- instructions\n- expected output contract\n- required frontmatter fields\n\nBuilders exist for:\n- `analyze-workflow`\n- `design-pipeline`\n- `synthesize-spec`\n- `brainstorm-gaps`\n- `panel-review`\n\n### Per-step output artifacts\n- step 1: `validate-config-result.json`\n- step 2: `component-inventory.md`\n- step 3: `portify-analysis.md`\n- step 4: `portify-spec.md`\n- step 5: `synthesized-spec.md`\n- step 6: `brainstorm-gaps.md`\n- step 7:\n  - `panel-review.md`\n  - `panel-report.md`\n\n## 5. How steps report status\n\nStatus reporting happens primarily through `PortifyStepResult`.\n\n### Common reporting fields set by steps\nEvery step returns a `PortifyStepResult` with some or all of:\n- `portify_status`\n- `step_name`\n- `step_number`\n- `phase`\n- `artifact_path`\n- `gate_tier`\n- `iteration_number` for iterative steps\n- `review_required`\n- `review_accepted`\n- `failure_classification`\n\n### Status patterns by step\n\n#### Step 1 `validate-config`\nReturns:\n- `PASS` if valid\n- `FAIL` if invalid\n\nGate tier:\n- `EXEMPT`\n\nArtifact:\n- `validate-config-result.json`\n\n#### Step 2 `discover-components`\nReturns:\n- always `PASS` on successful execution\n- no explicit internal failure branches other than filesystem write problems surfacing naturally\n\nGate tier:\n- `STANDARD`\n\nArtifact:\n- `component-inventory.md`\n\n#### Step 3 `analyze-workflow`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if inventory missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on non-zero subprocess exit\n- `FAIL` on SC-003 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nGate tier:\n- `STRICT`\n\n#### Step 4 `design-pipeline`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if prior analysis missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `SKIPPED` if `config.dry_run` triggers halt after this step\n- `FAIL` with `USER_REJECTION` if review denied\n- `FAIL` on SC-004 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nFields:\n- `review_required`\n- `review_accepted`\n\n#### Step 5 `synthesize-spec`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if template or required prior artifacts missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- retries sentinel cleanup up to 2 times\n- `FAIL` with `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT` if placeholders remain after retries\n- `FAIL` on SC-005 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nIteration field:\n- `iteration_number=attempt`\n\n#### Step 6 `brainstorm-gaps`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if synthesized spec missing\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `FAIL` on SC-006 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\n#### Step 7 `panel-review`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if prerequisites missing\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `FAIL` if additive-only section hashing validation fails\n- convergence can end in converged or escalated internally\n- `FAIL` with `USER_REJECTION` if final user review rejects\n- `FAIL` on SC-007 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nFields:\n- `iteration_number = completed iterations`\n- `review_required = True`\n- `review_accepted = True/False`\n\n## 6. Existing gate infrastructure\n\nFiles:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/gates.py`\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/steps/gates.py`\n\n### Step 1-2 gates (`steps/gates.py`)\n\n#### `VALIDATE_CONFIG_GATE`\n- `required_frontmatter_fields=[]`\n- `min_lines=0`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"EXEMPT\"`\n\n`gate_validate_config(result, timing_limit=1.0)`\nChecks:\n- advisory timing under 1s\n- consistency:\n  - valid => no errors\n  - invalid => errors present\n\nReturns `tuple[bool, str]`\n\n#### `DISCOVER_COMPONENTS_GATE`\n- required frontmatter:\n  - `source_skill`\n  - `component_count`\n- `min_lines=5`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\"`\n\n`gate_discover_components(...)`\nChecks:\n- artifact exists\n- YAML frontmatter exists\n- required fields present\n- `component_count` is non-negative int\n- `total_lines` if present is non-negative int\n- advisory timing under 5s\n\n### Step 3-7 gates (`gates.py`)\n\n#### `ANALYZE_WORKFLOW_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `component_count`\n- `analysis_sections`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=20`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: at least 5 sections\n\n#### `DESIGN_PIPELINE_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `pipeline_steps`\n- `gate_count`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=30`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic checks:\n  - at least 5 frontmatter fields\n  - data flow diagram present via code block or arrows\n\n#### `SYNTHESIZE_SPEC_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `synthesis_version`\n- `placeholder_count`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=15`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: no `{{SC_PLACEHOLDER:*}}`\n\n#### `BRAINSTORM_GAPS_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `gaps_found`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=10`\n- `STANDARD`\n\n#### `PANEL_REVIEW_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `iteration`\n- `convergence_state`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=15`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: `convergence_state` must be terminal:\n  - `converged`\n  - `blocked`\n\n### Registry\n`GATE_REGISTRY` maps every step name to its `GateCriteria`.\n\nThis is the core step registry for gate logic:\n- `validate-config`\n- `discover-components`\n- `analyze-workflow`\n- `design-pipeline`\n- `synthesize-spec`\n- `brainstorm-gaps`\n- `panel-review`\n\n## 7. Monitoring and TUI status\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/monitor.py`\n\n### What exists\nThere is monitoring infrastructure, but not a real TUI renderer.\n\nExisting pieces:\n\n#### `EventRecord`\nFields:\n- `event_type`\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `timestamp`\n- `data`\n\nSerialized JSON keys:\n- `event`\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `ts`\n- plus any extra `data`\n\n#### `EventLogger`\nPurpose:\n- writes NDJSON line-per-event output\n- stores events in memory\n\nMethods:\n- `emit(event_type, step=\"\", phase=0, **data)`\n- `events` property\n- `get_output()`\n\n#### `StepTiming`\nFields:\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n\nProperty:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n#### `PhaseTiming`\nFields:\n- `phase`\n- `name`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n- `step_timings`\n\nProperty:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n#### `TimingCapture`\nTracks:\n- pipeline start/end\n- step start/end\n- phase timing accumulation\n\nMethods:\n- `start_pipeline()`\n- `end_pipeline()`\n- `start_step(step, phase=0)`\n- `end_step(step)`\n- `get_step_timing(step)`\n- `get_phase_timing(phase)`\n\nProperties:\n- `total_duration`\n- `step_timings`\n- `phase_timings`\n\n#### Failure classification\n`classify_failure(...)` maps a failing situation into one of the 7 failure classes in priority order:\n1. `USER_REJECTION`\n2. `BUDGET_EXHAUSTION`\n3. `TIMEOUT`\n4. `MISSING_ARTIFACT`\n5. `MALFORMED_FRONTMATTER`\n6. `GATE_FAILURE`\n7. `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT`\n\nNotable heuristics:\n- missing artifact if expected path absent\n- malformed frontmatter if content exists but does not start with `---`\n- partial artifact if content contains `{{SC_PLACEHOLDER:...}}`\n\n#### Diagnostic report generation\n`generate_diagnostic_report(...)` produces markdown containing:\n- summary\n- per-step result table\n- phase timing table\n- event summary counts\n\n### What does not exist\nI did not find:\n- a curses/rich/live terminal UI\n- a render loop\n- progress bar or table renderer\n- code that updates `PortifyMonitorState` live\n- code integrating `EventLogger`, `TimingCapture`, and `PortifyMonitorState` into the top-level runner\n\nSo there is monitoring data infrastructure, but not an implemented TUI.\n\n## 8. Convergence and iteration logic\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/convergence.py`\n\n### State machine\n`ConvergenceState`:\n- `RUNNING`\n- `CONVERGED`\n- `ESCALATED`\n\nTerminal states:\n- `CONVERGED`\n- `ESCALATED`\n\n### Escalation reasons\n`EscalationReason`:\n- `MAX_ITERATIONS`\n- `BUDGET_EXHAUSTED`\n- `USER_REJECTED`\n\n### `IterationResult`\nFields:\n- `iteration: int = 0`\n- `unaddressed_criticals: int = 0`\n- `quality_scores: dict[str, float] = {}`\n- `content: str = \"\"`\n\nComputed:\n- `overall_score`\n  - mean of:\n    - clarity\n    - completeness\n    - testability\n    - consistency\n\n### Budget abstraction\n`BudgetGuard` protocol:\n- `has_budget(estimated_cost)`\n- `remaining_budget()`\n\n`SimpleBudgetGuard` fields:\n- `total_budget: float = 100.0`\n- `spent: float = 0.0`\n- `per_iteration_cost: float = 10.0`\n\nMethods:\n- `has_budget`\n- `remaining_budget`\n- `record_spend`\n\n### `ConvergenceResult`\nFields:\n- `state: ConvergenceState = RUNNING`\n- `iterations_completed: int = 0`\n- `last_result: IterationResult | None = None`\n- `escalation_reason: EscalationReason | None = None`\n- `quality_scores: dict[str, float] = {}`\n\nComputed:\n- `overall_score`\n- `is_converged`\n- `is_escalated`\n\n### `ConvergenceEngine`\nCore behavior:\n- takes `max_iterations`\n- optional `budget_guard`\n- stores submitted iteration results\n- state starts as `RUNNING`\n\nMethods:\n- `is_done`\n- `current_iteration`\n- `state`\n- `check_budget(estimated_cost=None)`\n- `submit(iteration_result)`\n- `escalate_budget()`\n- `escalate_user()`\n- `result()`\n\n### Convergence predicate\nOn `submit(iteration_result)`:\n1. if `unaddressed_criticals == 0`\n   - state becomes `CONVERGED`\n2. else if iterations reached `max_iterations`\n   - state becomes `ESCALATED`\n   - reason `MAX_ITERATIONS`\n3. else\n   - state remains `RUNNING`\n\n### How step 7 uses it\nIn `panel_review.py`:\n- initializes `SimpleBudgetGuard(total_budget=config.max_convergence * 2.0, per_iteration_cost=1.0)`\n- checks budget before each iteration\n- each iteration runs one Claude subprocess\n- parses scores and critical counts from output\n- submits `IterationResult` to engine\n- if out of budget: `engine.escalate_budget()`\n- after convergence loop:\n  - generates panel report\n  - prompts final user review\n  - if user rejects: `engine.escalate_user()`\n\n## 9. Step registry and names in `steps/__init__.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/steps/__init__.py`\n\nExports these step functions:\n- `run_validate_config`\n- `run_discover_components`\n- `run_analyze_workflow`\n- `run_design_pipeline`\n- `run_synthesize_spec`\n- `run_brainstorm_gaps`\n- `run_panel_review`\n\nAlso exports:\n- `scan_sentinels`\n- `gate_validate_config`\n- `gate_discover_components`\n- `VALIDATE_CONFIG_GATE`\n- `DISCOVER_COMPONENTS_GATE`\n\n### Practical step order\nThe order implied across docstrings, step numbers, and contracts is:\n\n1. `validate-config`\n2. `discover-components`\n3. `analyze-workflow`\n4. `design-pipeline`\n5. `synthesize-spec`\n6. `brainstorm-gaps`\n7. `panel-review`\n\nThere is no separate central list constant in `steps/__init__.py`, but this order is consistent everywhere else.\n\n## 10. Existing failure handling\n\nThere is quite a bit already implemented.\n\n### Failure types supported\nFrom `FailureClassification`:\n- timeout\n- missing_artifact\n- malformed_frontmatter\n- gate_failure\n- user_rejection\n- budget_exhaustion\n- partial_artifact\n\n### Step-level failure handling patterns\nCommon patterns:\n- fail fast on missing prerequisite artifacts\n- timeout classification when subprocess exit indicates timeout\n- subprocess non-zero exit => fail\n- gate failure => fail\n- user review rejection => fail with `USER_REJECTION`\n\n### Notable specialized handling\n\n#### Step 4 `design-pipeline`\n- dry-run early exit emits dry-run contract and returns `SKIPPED`\n- explicit interactive review gate\n- rejection classified as `USER_REJECTION`\n\n#### Step 5 `synthesize-spec`\n- special fail-fast if template missing\n- sentinel scan with retry loop\n- remaining placeholders after retries => `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT`\n\n#### Step 7 `panel-review`\n- additive-only enforcement via section hashing\n- budget exhaustion escalates convergence engine\n- user rejection escalates convergence engine and returns failure\n- downstream readiness is calculated but not itself used as a hard failing return condition; it is reported\n\n### Monitoring-side classifier\n`monitor.py` has `classify_failure(...)` that can infer classification from:\n- timeout flag\n- artifact existence\n- frontmatter\n- gate pass result\n- user rejection\n- budget exhaustion\n\nThis suggests the intended orchestration layer should centralize failure classification instead of relying only on per-step hardcoded classifications.\n\n## 11. Existing resume and review logic\n\n### Resume logic\nResume support exists conceptually, but the top-level runner does not yet implement it.\n\nExisting resume-related pieces:\n- CLI flag `--start`\n- config field `start_step`\n- `ResumeContext` model\n- `PortifyStepResult.is_resumable`\n- contract resume generation in `generate_resume_command(...)`\n- resumable steps hardcoded as:\n  - `synthesize-spec`\n  - `brainstorm-gaps`\n  - `panel-review`\n\nCurrent limitations:\n- `cli.py` does not yet execute steps based on `start_step`\n- step implementations do not populate detailed `resume_context`\n- no pipeline executor currently reconstructs state from prior artifacts\n\n### Review logic\nThere are two real review gates today:\n\n#### Step 4 review gate\nIn `design_pipeline.py`:\n- unless `skip_review=True`\n- prompts on stderr:\n  - review generated artifact\n  - answer `y/n`\n- rejection => `FAIL`, `review_required=True`, `review_accepted=False`, classification `USER_REJECTION`\n\n#### Step 7 review gate\nIn `panel_review.py`:\n- final acceptance prompt:\n  - `Accept panel review result? [y/N]:`\n- `skip_review=True` auto-accepts\n- rejection escalates convergence state to user rejected and returns failure\n\nSo `--skip-review` is already meaningful in step code, even though the top-level runner is not yet invoking those steps.\n\n## 12. The current codebase already has:\n\n- typed config and step result models\n- gate infrastructure for all 7 steps\n- contract builders for success/partial/failure/dry-run\n- Claude subprocess wrapper for steps 3-7\n- monitoring primitives: NDJSON event logging, timing capture, failure classification, markdown diagnostic reporting\n- convergence engine for step 7 iterations\n- step implementations for all 7 steps\n- prompt builders for all Claude-assisted steps\n\nWhat is missing at the top level is the orchestration layer that actually sequences steps 1-7, tracks overall status, invokes contract emission on exits, and integrates monitor/timing/event logger in a single execution loop.\n\n## 1. Data models in `models.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/models.py`\n\n### Imported shared pipeline types\nThis module imports these shared base types from `superclaude.cli.pipeline.models`:\n- `PipelineConfig`\n- `StepResult`\n- `StepStatus`\n\nImportant: `StepStatus` itself is not defined in cli_portify. It is imported from the shared pipeline package.\n\n### Enums\n\n#### `PortifyStatus`\nStep-level status enum:\n- `PENDING = \"pending\"`\n- `RUNNING = \"running\"`\n- `PASS = \"pass\"`\n- `FAIL = \"fail\"`\n- `TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"`\n- `SKIPPED = \"skipped\"`\n- `ERROR = \"error\"`\n\nThis is the primary cli_portify step status vocabulary.\n\n#### `PortifyOutcome`\nAggregate pipeline outcome enum:\n- `SUCCESS = \"success\"`\n- `PARTIAL = \"partial\"`\n- `FAILED = \"failed\"`\n- `DRY_RUN = \"dry_run\"`\n\nThis concept aligns with contract emission status, though `contract.py` defines its own `ContractStatus` enum separately.\n\n#### `FailureClassification`\nFailure taxonomy used for diagnostics and resume logic:\n- `TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"`\n- `MISSING_ARTIFACT = \"missing_artifact\"`\n- `MALFORMED_FRONTMATTER = \"malformed_frontmatter\"`\n- `GATE_FAILURE = \"gate_failure\"`\n- `USER_REJECTION = \"user_rejection\"`\n- `BUDGET_EXHAUSTION = \"budget_exhaustion\"`\n- `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT = \"partial_artifact\"`\n\n### `PortifyConfig`\nExtends shared `PipelineConfig`.\n\nFields:\n- `workflow_path: Path = Path(\".\")`\n- `output_dir: Path = Path(\".\")`\n- `cli_name: str = \"\"`\n- `skip_review: bool = False`\n- `start_step: str | None = None`\n- `iteration_timeout: int = 300`\n- `max_convergence: int = 3`\n\nInherited fields are not listed here explicitly, but `config.py` passes these into it via the base class:\n- `work_dir`\n- `dry_run`\n- `max_turns`\n- `model`\n- `debug`\n\nKey behavior:\n- `__post_init__`: if `work_dir` is empty or `\".\"`, it sets `work_dir = output_dir`\n- `resolve_workflow_path()`: validates workflow path and requires `SKILL.md`\n- `derive_cli_name()`: derives CLI name from folder name by:\n  - stripping `sc-` prefix\n  - stripping `-protocol` suffix\n  - replacing `_` with `-`\n- `check_output_writable()`: creates output dir if needed and validates it is a directory\n- `check_name_collision(existing_commands=None)`: checks built-in command collisions against:\n  - `install`\n  - `mcp`\n  - `update`\n  - `install-skill`\n  - `doctor`\n  - `version`\n  - `sprint`\n  - `roadmap`\n  - `cleanup-audit`\n  - `tasklist`\n- `to_snake_case(name=None)`: kebab to snake conversion\n- `results_dir` property: `output_dir / \"results\"`\n- `artifacts_dir` property: `output_dir / \"artifacts\"`\n\n### `ResumeContext`\nTyped resume metadata.\n\nFields:\n- `last_completed_step: str = \"\"`\n- `last_completed_step_number: int = 0`\n- `failed_step: str = \"\"`\n- `failed_step_number: int = 0`\n- `failure_classification: FailureClassification | None = None`\n- `re_run_required: bool = False`\n- `artifacts_preserved: list[str] = []`\n- `resume_command: str = \"\"`\n\nThis is present in the step result model, but current step implementations do not populate it much yet.\n\n### `PortifyStepResult`\nExtends shared `StepResult`.\n\nFields:\n- `portify_status: PortifyStatus = PortifyStatus.PENDING`\n- `step_name: str = \"\"`\n- `step_number: int = 0`\n- `phase: int = 0`\n- `artifact_path: str = \"\"`\n- `gate_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n- `iteration_timeout: int = 300`\n- `iteration_number: int = 0`\n- `review_required: bool = False`\n- `review_accepted: bool | None = None`\n- `failure_classification: FailureClassification | None = None`\n- `resume_context: ResumeContext = ResumeContext()`\n\nComputed property:\n- `is_resumable`\n  - returns `False` for `USER_REJECTION`\n  - otherwise returns `True` when status is `FAIL`, `TIMEOUT`, or `ERROR`\n\nSo current resumability logic is classification-based and intentionally excludes user rejection.\n\n### `ComponentEntry`\nRepresents one discovered workflow component.\n\nFields:\n- `name: str`\n- `path: str`\n- `component_type: str`\n- `line_count: int`\n\n### `ComponentInventory`\nProduced by step 2.\n\nFields:\n- `source_skill: str = \"\"`\n- `components: list[ComponentEntry] = []`\n\nComputed properties:\n- `component_count`\n- `total_lines`\n\n### `PortifyMonitorState`\nLive execution state intended for TUI rendering.\n\nFields:\n- `output_bytes: int = 0`\n- `output_bytes_prev: int = 0`\n- `last_growth_time: float = 0.0`\n- `last_event_time: float = 0.0`\n- `step_started_at: float = 0.0`\n- `events_received: int = 0`\n- `lines_total: int = 0`\n- `growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0`\n- `stall_seconds: float = 0.0`\n- `current_step: str = \"\"`\n- `current_iteration: int = 0`\n\nComputed property:\n- `stall_status`\n  - Contract architecture in `contract.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/contract.py`\n\n### Contract status enum\n`ContractStatus`:\n- `SUCCESS`\n- output keys:\n- `status`\n- `phases`\n- `artifacts`\n- `resume_command`\n- `timing`\n- `step_timings`\n- `gate_results`\n- `error_message`\n\n`__post_init__` populates default phases if omitted.\n\n### Default phases\nThe contract hardcodes 4 conceptual phases:\n\n1. `config-validation` — `steps_total=2`\n2. `workflow-analysis` — `steps_total=2`\n3. `spec-synthesis` — `steps_total=1`\n4. `review-convergence` — `steps_total=2`\n\nStep-to-phase mapping:\n- step 1 `validate-config` -> phase 1\n- step 2 `discover-components` -> phase 1\n- step 3 `analyze-workflow` -> phase 2\n- step 4 `design-pipeline` -> phase 2\n- step 5 `synthesize-spec` -> phase 3\n- step 6 `brainstorm-gaps` -> phase 4\n- step 7 `panel-review` -> phase 4\n\n### Contract builder functions\n\n#### `build_success_contract(...)`\nMarks all phases:\n- `status = \"completed\"`\n- `steps_completed = steps_total`\n\nSets:\n- `status = success`\n- `resume_command = \"\"`\n- `timing = {\"total_seconds\": total_duration}`\n\n#### `build_partial_contract(...)`\nUsed for escalated partial completion.\n\nInputs:\n- `step_results`\n- `artifacts`\n- `step_timings`\n- `gate_results`\n- `total_duration`\n- `resume_step=\"\"`\n\nBehavior:\n- builds phase states from step results\n- optionally generates resume command\n\n#### `build_failed_contract(...)`\nUsed for failure exit paths.\n\nAdds:\n- `error_message`\n- optional `resume_command`\n\nThis is intended to satisfy the \"no null contract on failure\" rule.\n\n#### `build_dry_run_contract(...)`\nSpecial dry-run behavior:\n- phases 1-2 marked `completed`\n- phases 3-4 marked `skipped`\n- `resume_command = \"\"`\n\nNote: comment says phases 1-2 are \"config validation + deterministic steps\", but implementation is based on conceptual pipeline phases, not actual execution tracking.\n\n### Resume command generation\n`RESUMABLE_STEPS`:\n- `synthesize-spec` -> 5\n- `brainstorm-gaps` -> 6\n- `panel-review` -> 7\n\n`generate_resume_command(failed_step, suggested_budget=None)` returns:\n- `superclaude cli-portify run <workflow_path> --start {failed_step}`\n- appends `--max-convergence {suggested_budget}` when provided\n\nNon-resumable steps return empty string.\n\n## 3. CLI entry point and flags in `cli.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/cli.py`\n\n### CLI group\n- Click group name: `cli-portify`\n\n### Command\n- Subcommand: `run`\n\n### Positional argument\n- `workflow_path` as `click.Path(exists=True)`\n\n### Defined flags\n- `--output` / stored as `output_dir`\n  - output directory for generated artifacts\n- `--cli-name`\n  - overrides derived CLI command name\n- `--dry-run`\n  - validates and plans without executing Claude steps\n  - help text says halts after step 2\n- `--skip-review`\n  - skips interactive review gates\n- `--start` / stored as `start_step`\n  - resume from a specific step\n  - help example: `synthesize-spec`\n- `--max-convergence`\n  - default `3`\n  - maximum convergence iterations for panel review\n- `--iteration-timeout`\n  - default `300`\n  - per-iteration timeout\n- `--max-turns`\n  - default `100`\n  - max turns per Claude subprocess\n- `--model`\n  - default empty string\n- `--debug`\n  - flag\n\n### Current actual behavior\nThe runner currently does only this:\n1. builds config via `load_portify_config(...)`\n2. validates config via `validate_portify_config(config)`\n3. if validation errors exist:\n   - prints each as `Error: ...`\n   - exits `1`\n4. if `dry_run`:\n   - prints a dry-run execution plan\n   - returns\n5. otherwise:\n   - prints `cli-portify: pipeline execution not yet implemented (start=...)`\n   - exits `0`\n\nSo:\n- `--start` exists but is not yet wired to an execution loop\n- `--skip-review` exists and is carried in config, but top-level orchestration is not using it yet\n- actual pipeline sequencing is still deferred\n\n### Dry-run display\n`_print_dry_run(config)` prints:\n- workflow path\n- derived CLI name\n- output dir\n- total step count: `7 (Steps 3-7 require Claude)`\n- max convergence\n- iteration timeout\n\n## 4. Pipeline execution flow\n\nThere is no fully implemented top-level pipeline runner yet in `cli.py`, but the intended flow is very clear from the steps, contracts, gates, prompts, and convergence code.\n\n### Intended step order\nFrom `steps/__init__.py` and step implementations:\n\n1. `validate-config`\n2. `discover-components`\n3. `analyze-workflow`\n4. `design-pipeline`\n5. `synthesize-spec`\n6. `brainstorm-gaps`\n7. `panel-review`\n\n### Phase grouping\n- Phase 1:\n  - step 1 `validate-config`\n  - step 2 `discover-components`\n- Phase 2:\n  - step 3 `analyze-workflow`\n  - step 4 `design-pipeline`\n- Phase 3:\n  - step 5 `synthesize-spec`\n- Phase 4:\n  - step 6 `brainstorm-gaps`\n  - step 7 `panel-review`\n\n### Step dependencies\n- Step 1 validates config and environment\n- Step 2 consumes resolved workflow path and inventories source files\n- Step 3 requires `component-inventory.md`\n- Step 4 requires `portify-analysis.md`, also references `component-inventory.md`\n- Step 5 requires:\n  - `release-spec-template.md`\n  - `portify-analysis.md`\n  - `portify-spec.md`\n- Step 6 requires `synthesized-spec.md`\n- Step 7 requires:\n  - `synthesized-spec.md`\n  - `brainstorm-gaps.md`\n\n### Claude-assisted vs deterministic\nDeterministic:\n- step 1\n- step 2\n\nClaude-assisted:\n- steps 3-7\n\n### Actual subprocess orchestration in `process.py`\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/process.py`\n\n`PortifyProcess` is not a pipeline executor. It is a step-level subprocess wrapper around shared `ClaudeProcess`.\n\nWhat it adds:\n- dual `--add-dir` scoping:\n  - `work_dir`\n  - `workflow_path` if different\n- prompt augmentation with `@absolute/path` references to prior artifacts\n- captured stdout/stderr/timeout/duration result object\n\n`ProcessResult` fields:\n- `exit_code`\n- `stdout_text`\n- `stderr_text`\n- `timed_out`\n- `duration_seconds`\n- `output_file`\n- `error_file`\n\n`succeeded` means:\n- `exit_code == 0`\n- and not timed out\n\n### Prompt construction flow\nAll Claude-assisted steps use `prompts.py` builders with a shared `PromptContext`.\n\nEach builder supplies:\n- referenced input artifacts\n- instructions\n- expected output contract\n- required frontmatter fields\n\nBuilders exist for:\n- `analyze-workflow`\n- `design-pipeline`\n- `synthesize-spec`\n- `brainstorm-gaps`\n- `panel-review`\n\n### Per-step output artifacts\n- step 1: `validate-config-result.json`\n- step 2: `component-inventory.md`\n- step 3: `portify-analysis.md`\n- step 4: `portify-spec.md`\n- step 5: `synthesized-spec.md`\n- step 6: `brainstorm-gaps.md`\n- step 7:\n  - `panel-review.md`\n  - `panel-report.md`\n\n## 5. How steps report status\n\nStatus reporting happens primarily through `PortifyStepResult`.\n\n### Common reporting fields set by steps\nEvery step returns a `PortifyStepResult` with some or all of:\n- `portify_status`\n- `step_name`\n- `step_number`\n- `phase`\n- `artifact_path`\n- `gate_tier`\n- `iteration_number` for iterative steps\n- `review_required`\n- `review_accepted`\n- `failure_classification`\n\n### Status patterns by step\n\n#### Step 1 `validate-config`\nReturns:\n- `PASS` if valid\n- `FAIL` if invalid\n\nGate tier:\n- `EXEMPT`\n\nArtifact:\n- `validate-config-result.json`\n\n#### Step 2 `discover-components`\nReturns:\n- always `PASS` on successful execution\n- no explicit internal failure branches other than filesystem write problems surfacing naturally\n\nGate tier:\n- `STANDARD`\n\nArtifact:\n- `component-inventory.md`\n\n#### Step 3 `analyze-workflow`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if inventory missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on non-zero subprocess exit\n- `FAIL` on SC-003 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nGate tier:\n- `STRICT`\n\n#### Step 4 `design-pipeline`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if prior analysis missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `SKIPPED` if `config.dry_run` triggers halt after this step\n- `FAIL` with `USER_REJECTION` if review denied\n- `FAIL` on SC-004 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nFields:\n- `review_required`\n- `review_accepted`\n\n#### Step 5 `synthesize-spec`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if template or required prior artifacts missing\n- `TIMEOUT` on subprocess timeout\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- retries sentinel cleanup up to 2 times\n- `FAIL` with `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT` if placeholders remain after retries\n- `FAIL` on SC-005 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nIteration field:\n- `iteration_number=attempt`\n\n#### Step 6 `brainstorm-gaps`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if synthesized spec missing\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `FAIL` on SC-006 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\n#### Step 7 `panel-review`\nReturns:\n- `FAIL` with `MISSING_ARTIFACT` if prerequisites missing\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `FAIL` on subprocess failure\n- `FAIL` if additive-only section hashing validation fails\n- convergence can end in converged or escalated internally\n- `FAIL` with `USER_REJECTION` if final user review rejects\n- `FAIL` on SC-007 gate failure\n- `PASS` on success\n\nFields:\n- `iteration_number = completed iterations`\n- `review_required = True`\n- `review_accepted = True/False`\n\n## 6. Existing gate infrastructure\n\nFiles:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/gates.py`\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/steps/gates.py`\n\n### Step 1-2 gates (`steps/gates.py`)\n\n#### `VALIDATE_CONFIG_GATE`\n- `required_frontmatter_fields=[]`\n- `min_lines=0`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"EXEMPT\"`\n\n`gate_validate_config(result, timing_limit=1.0)`\nChecks:\n- advisory timing under 1s\n- consistency:\n  - valid => no errors\n  - invalid => errors present\n\nReturns `tuple[bool, str]`\n\n#### `DISCOVER_COMPONENTS_GATE`\n- required frontmatter:\n  - `source_skill`\n  - `component_count`\n- `min_lines=5`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\"`\n\n`gate_discover_components(...)`\nChecks:\n- artifact exists\n- YAML frontmatter exists\n- required fields present\n- `component_count` is non-negative int\n- `total_lines` if present is non-negative int\n- advisory timing under 5s\n\n### Step 3-7 gates (`gates.py`)\n\n#### `ANALYZE_WORKFLOW_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `component_count`\n- `analysis_sections`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=20`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: at least 5 sections\n\n#### `DESIGN_PIPELINE_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `pipeline_steps`\n- `gate_count`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=30`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic checks:\n  - at least 5 frontmatter fields\n  - data flow diagram present via code block or arrows\n\n#### `SYNTHESIZE_SPEC_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `synthesis_version`\n- `placeholder_count`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=15`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: no `{{SC_PLACEHOLDER:*}}`\n\n#### `BRAINSTORM_GAPS_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `gaps_found`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=10`\n- `STANDARD`\n\n#### `PANEL_REVIEW_GATE`\nRequired frontmatter:\n- `step`\n- `source_skill`\n- `cli_name`\n- `iteration`\n- `convergence_state`\n\nOther rules:\n- `min_lines=15`\n- `STRICT`\n- semantic check: `convergence_state` must be terminal:\n  - `converged`\n  - `blocked`\n\n### Registry\n`GATE_REGISTRY` maps every step name to its `GateCriteria`.\n\nThis is the core step registry for gate logic:\n- `validate-config`\n- `discover-components`\n- `analyze-workflow`\n- `design-pipeline`\n- `synthesize-spec`\n- `brainstorm-gaps`\n- `panel-review`\n\n## 7. Monitoring and TUI status\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/monitor.py`\n\n### What exists\nThere is monitoring infrastructure, but not a real TUI renderer.\n\nExisting pieces:\n\n#### `EventRecord`\nFields:\n- `event_type`\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `timestamp`\n- `data`\n\nSerialized JSON keys:\n- `event`\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `ts`\n- plus any extra `data`\n\n#### `EventLogger`\nPurpose:\n- writes NDJSON line-per-event output\n- stores events in memory\n\nMethods:\n- `emit(event_type, step=\"\", phase=0, **data)`\n- `events` property\n- `get_output()`\n\n#### `StepTiming`\nFields:\n- `step`\n- `phase`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n\nProperty:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n#### `PhaseTiming`\nFields:\n- `phase`\n- `name`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n- `step_timings`\n\nProperty:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n#### `TimingCapture`\nTracks:\n- pipeline start/end\n- step start/end\n- phase timing accumulation\n\nMethods:\n- `start_pipeline()`\n- `end_pipeline()`\n- `start_step(step, phase=0)`\n- `end_step(step)`\n- `get_step_timing(step)`\n- `get_phase_timing(phase)`\n\nProperties:\n- `total_duration`\n- `step_timings`\n- `phase_timings`\n\n#### Failure classification\n`classify_failure(...)` maps a failing situation into one of the 7 failure classes in priority order:\n1. `USER_REJECTION`\n2. `BUDGET_EXHAUSTION`\n3. `TIMEOUT`\n4. `MISSING_ARTIFACT`\n5. `MALFORMED_FRONTMATTER`\n6. `GATE_FAILURE`\n7. `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT`\n\nNotable heuristics:\n- missing artifact if expected path absent\n- malformed frontmatter if content exists but does not start with `---`\n- partial artifact if content contains `{{SC_PLACEHOLDER:...}}`\n\n#### Diagnostic report generation\n`generate_diagnostic_report(...)` produces markdown containing:\n- summary\n- per-step result table\n- phase timing table\n- event summary counts\n\n### What does not exist\nI did not `PortifyMonitorState` into the top-level runner\n\nSo there is monitoring data infrastructure, but not an implemented TUI.\n\n## 8. Convergence and iteration logic\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/convergence.py`\n\n### State machine\n`ConvergenceState`:\n- `RUNNING`\n- `CONVERGED`\n- `ESCALATED`\n\nTerminal states:\n- `CONVERGED`\n- `ESCALATED`\n\n### Escalation reasons\n`EscalationReason`:\n- `MAX_ITERATIONS`\n- `BUDGET_EXHAUSTED`\n- `USER_REJECTED`\n\n### `IterationResult`\nFields:\n- `iteration: int = 0`\n- `unaddressed_criticals: int = 0`\n- `quality_scores: dict[str, float] = {}`\n- `content: str = \"\"`\n\nComputed:\n- `overall_score`\n  - mean of:\n    - clarity\n    - completeness\n    - testability\n    - consistency\n\n### Budget abstraction\n`BudgetGuard` protocol:\n- `has_budget(estimated_cost)`\n- `remaining_budget()`\n\n`SimpleBudgetGuard` fields:\n- `total_budget: float = 100.0`\n- `spent: float = 0.0`\n- `per_iteration_cost: float = 10.0`\n\nMethods:\n- `has_budget`\n- `remaining_budget`\n- `record_spend`\n\n### `ConvergenceResult`\nFields:\n- `state: ConvergenceState = RUNNING`\n- `iterations_completed: int = 0`\n- `last_result: IterationResult | None = None`\n- `escalation_reason: EscalationReason | None = None`\n- `quality_scores: dict[str, float] = {}`\n\nComputed:\n- `overall_score`\n- `is_converged`\n- `is_escalated`\n\n### `ConvergenceEngine`\nCore behavior:\n- takes `max_iterations`\n- optional `budget_guard`\n- stores submitted iteration results\n- state starts as `RUNNING`\n\nMethods:\n- `is_done`\n- `current_iteration`\n- `state`\n- `check_budget(estimated_cost=None)`\n- `submit(iteration_result)`\n- `escalate_budget()`\n- `escalate_user()`\n- `result()`\n\n### Convergence predicate\nOn `submit(iteration_result)`:\n1. if `unaddressed_criticals == 0`\n   - state becomes `CONVERGED`\n2. else if iterations reached `max_iterations`\n   - state becomes `ESCALATED`\n   - reason `MAX_ITERATIONS`\n3. else\n   - state remains `RUNNING`\n\n### How step 7 uses it\nIn `panel_review.py`:\n- initializes `SimpleBudgetGuard(total_budget=config.max_convergence * 2.0, per_iteration_cost=1.0)`\n- checks budget before each iteration\n- each iteration runs one Claude subprocess\n- parses scores and critical counts from output\n- submits `IterationResult` to engine\n- if out of budget: `engine.escalate_budget()`\n- after convergence loop:\n  - generates panel report\n  - prompts final user review\n  - if user rejects: `engine.escalate_user()`\n\n## 9. Step registry and names in `steps/__init__.py`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/cli_portify/steps/__init__.py`\n\nExports these step functions:\n- `run_validate_config`\n- `run_discover_components`\n- `run_analyze_workflow`\n- `run_design_pipeline`\n- `run_synthesize_spec`\n- `run_brainstorm_gaps`\n- `run_panel_review`\n\nAlso exports:\n- `scan_sentinels`\n- `gate_validate_config`\n- `gate_discover_components`\n- `VALIDATE_CONFIG_GATE`\n- `DISCOVER_COMPONENTS_GATE`\n\n### Practical step order\nThe order implied across docstrings, step numbers, and contracts is:\n\n1. `validate-config`\n2. `discover-components`\n3. `analyze-workflow`\n4. `design-pipeline`\n5. `synthesize-spec`\n6. `brainstorm-gaps`\n7. `panel-review`\n\nThere is no separate central list constant in `steps/__init__.py`, but this order is consistent everywhere else.\n\n## 10. Existing failure handling\n\nThere is quite a bit already implemented.\n\n### Failure types supported\nFrom `FailureClassification`:\n- timeout\n- missing_artifact\n- malformed_frontmatter\n- gate_failure\n- user_rejection\n- budget_exhaustion\n- partial_artifact\n\n### Step-level failure handling patterns\nCommon patterns:\n- fail fast on missing prerequisite artifacts\n- timeout classification when subprocess exit indicates timeout\n- subprocess non-zero exit => fail\n- gate failure => fail\n- user review rejection => fail with `USER_REJECTION`\n\n### Notable specialized handling\n\n#### Step 4 `design-pipeline`\n- dry-run early exit emits dry-run contract and returns `SKIPPED`\n- explicit interactive review gate\n- rejection classified as `USER_REJECTION`\n\n#### Step 5 `synthesize-spec`\n- special fail-fast if template missing\n- sentinel scan with retry loop\n- remaining placeholders after retries => `PARTIAL_ARTIFACT`\n\n#### Step 7 `panel-review`\n- additive-only enforcement via section hashing\n- budget exhaustion escalates convergence engine\n- user rejection escalates convergence engine and returns failure\n- downstream readiness is calculated but not itself used as a hard failing return condition; it is reported\n\n### Monitoring-side classifier\n`monitor.py` has `classify_failure(...)` that can infer classification from:\n- timeout flag\n- artifact existence\n- frontmatter\n- gate pass result\n- user rejection\n- budget exhaustion\n\nThis suggests the intended orchestration layer should centralize failure classification instead of relying only on per-step hardcoded classifications.\n\n## 11. Handles: strings, integers, floats, booleans, and quoted strings.\n    Does not handle nested structures, lists, or multi-line values.\n    \"\"\"\n    result: dict[str, Any] = {}\n    for line in text.strip().splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith(\"#\"):\n            continue\n        if \":\" not in line:\n            continue\n        key, _, raw_val = line.partition(\":\")\n        key = key.strip()\n        val = raw_val.strip()\n        # Unquote\n        if (val.startswith('\"') and val.endswith('\"')) or (\n            val.startswith(\"'\") and val.endswith(\"'\")\n        ):\n            result[key] = val[1:-1]\n        elif val.lower() in (\"true\", \"yes\"):\n            result[key] = True\n        elif val.lower() in (\"false\", \"no\"):\n            result[key] = False\n        elif val.lower() in (\"null\", \"~\", \"\"):\n            result[key] = None\n        else:\n            # Try int, then float, then string\n            try:\n                result[key] = int(val)\n            except ValueError:\n                try:\n                    result[key] = float(val)\n                except ValueError:\n                    result[key] = val\n    return result\n\n\ndef validate_frontmatter_fields(\n    frontmatter: dict[str, Any],\n    required_fields: list[str],\n) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Validate that required frontmatter fields are present.\n\n    Args:\n        frontmatter: Parsed frontmatter dictionary.\n        required_fields: List of required field names.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of missing field names (empty if all present).\n    \"\"\"\n    return [f for f in required_fields if f not in frontmatter]\n\n\n# --- File Checks ---\n\n\ndef file_exists(path: Path | Used to verify additive-only changes: sections can be added but\n    existing sections must not be modified or removed.\n\n    Args:\n        content: Section text content.\n\n    Returns:\n        Hex-encoded SHA-256 hash string.\n    \"\"\"\n    normalized = content.strip()\n    return hashlib.sha256(normalized.encode(\"utf-8\")).hexdigest()\n\n\ndef extract_sections(content: str) -> dict[str, Markdown content (body, not frontmatter).\n\n    Returns:\n        Dict mapping heading text to section content.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: dict[str, str] = {}\n    current_heading = \"\"\n    current_lines: list[str] = []\n\n    for line in content.split(\"\\n\"):\n        if line.startswith(\"## \"):\n            # Save previous section\n            if current_heading:\n                sections[current_heading] = \"\\n\".join(current_lines)\n            current_heading = line[3:].strip()\n            current_lines = []\n        else:\n            current_lines.append(line)\n\n    # new_content: str,\n) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify that changes to a document are additive-only.\n\n    Checks that no existing section was modified or removed.\n    New sections may be added freely.\n\n    Args:\n        old_hashes: Mapping of section heading to previous hash.\n        new_content: New document body content.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of violation messages (empty if additive-only).\n    \"\"\"\n    new_sections = extract_sections(new_content)\n    violations: list[str] = []\n\n    for heading, old_hash in old_hashes.items():\n        if heading not in new_sections:\n            violations.append(f\"Section removed: '{heading}'\")\n        elif hash_section(new_sections[heading]) != old_hash:\n            violations.append(f\"Section modified: '{heading}'\")\n\n    return violations\n\n\n# --- Line Counting ---\n\n\ndef count_lines(path: Path | str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Count lines in a file.\n\n    Args:\n        path: Path to the file.\n\n table.add_row(\n            str(i),\n            step.name,\n            Text(label, style=style),\n            Text(gate_text, style=gate_style),\n            dur,\n            info,\n        )\n\n    # Footer with total elapsed\n    table.add_section()\n    elapsed_str = f\"{state.total_elapsed:.1f}s\"\n    table.add_row(\"\", \"Total elapsed\", \"\", \"\", elapsed_str, \"\")\n\n    return table\n\n\nclass TuiDashboard:\n    \"\"\"Rich TUI live dashboard for pipeline execution.\n\n    Renders a live-updating table showing step progress, gate results,\n    timing, iteration count, and warnings. Pauses display for review\n    gate prompts.\n\n    Falls back to simple stderr line output in non-terminal environments.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, state: DashboardState | None = None) -> None:\n        self._state = state or DashboardState()\n        self._live: Live | None = None\n        self._console: Console | None = None\n        self._is_terminal = HAS_RICH and hasattr(sys.stderr, \"isatty\") and sys.stderr.isatty()\n\n    @property\n    def state(self) -> DashboardState:\n        return self._state\n\n    @property\n    def is_live(self) -> bool:\n        return self._live is not None\n\n    def start(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Start the live dashboard display.\"\"\"\n        self._state.pipeline_start = time.time()\n        if not self._is_terminal:\n            return\n        self._console = Console(stderr=True)\n        self._live = Live(\n            _build_dashboard_table(self._state),\n            console=self._console,\n            refresh_per_second=2,\n            transient=True,\n        )\n        self._live.start()\n\n    def stop(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Stop the live dashboard and print final state.\"\"\"\n        self._state.compute_elapsed()\n        if self._live is not None:\n            self._live.stop()\n            self._live = None\n        if self._console is not None:\n            self._console.print(_build_dashboard_table(self._state))\n\n    def refresh(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Refresh the live display with current state.\"\"\"\n        self._state.compute_elapsed()\n        if self._live is not None:\n            self._live.update(_build_dashboard_table(self._state))\n        elif not self._is_terminal and self._state.current_step:\n            _fallback_status(self._state)\n\n    def step_start(self, step_name: str) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Mark a step as running and refresh.\"\"\"\n        self._state.mark_running(step_name)\n        self.refresh()\n\n    def step_complete(\n        self, step_name: str, status: str, duration: float, gate_result: str = \"\"\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Mark a step as complete and refresh.\"\"\"\n        self._state.mark_complete(step_name, status, duration, gate_result)\n        self.refresh()\n\n    def set_iteration(self, step_name: str, iteration: int) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Update the iteration counter for a step.\"\"\"\n        self._state.update_step(step_name, iteration=iteration)\n        self._state.current_iteration = iteration\n        self.refresh()\n\n    def pause_for_review(self, prompt: str) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Pause the live display for a review gate prompt.\"\"\"\n        self._state.set_review_pause(prompt)\n        if self._live is not None:\n            self._live.stop()\n            self._live = None\n\n    def resume_after_review(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Resume the live display after review gate completes.\"\"\"\n        self._state.clear_review_pause()\n        if self._is_terminal and self._console is not None:\n            self._live = Live(\n                _build_dashboard_table(self._state),\n                console=self._console,\n                refresh_per_second=2,\n                transient=True,\n            )\n            self._live.start()\n\n    def add_warning(self, warning: str) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Add a warning to the dashboard.\"\"\"\n        self._state.add_warning(warning)\n        self.refresh()\n\n\ndef _fallback_status(state: DashboardState) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print simple status line for non-terminal environments.\"\"\"\n    step = state.current_step\n    elapsed = f\"{state.total_elapsed:.1f}s\"\n    print(f\"[portify] {step} running... ({elapsed})\", file=sys.stderr)\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Missing template — fail-fast with clear error and remediation path\n2. Missing skills — graceful fallback with warning\n3. Malformed artifact — diagnostic classification and targeted retry\n4. Timeout — per-iteration and total budget handling\n5. Partial artifact — re-run policy (prefer re-run over trust)\n6. Non-writable output — early detection in validate-config\n7. Exhausted budget — ESCALATED terminal state with resume guidance\n\nPer D-0039 / R-027.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.models import (\n    FailureClassification,\n    PortifyStatus,\n    PortifyStepResult,\n    ResumeContext,\n)\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.resume import build_resume_command, is_resumable\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass FailureHandlerResult:\n    \"\"\"Result from a failure handler with message and remediation.\"\"\"\n\n    step_result: PortifyStepResult\n    error_message: str\n    remediation: str\n    is_terminal: bool\n\n\ndef handle_missing_template(\n    step_name: str,\n    step_number: int,\n    phase: int,\n    template_path: str,\n) -> FailureHandlerResult:\n    \"\"\"Handle missing template failure — fail-fast with remediation.\n\n    This is a non-recoverable configuration error.
